  254. The Olay Fresh Effects brush is unique in it's triangle-shaped head. Like an ultrasonic toothbrush (think Sonicare), this brush vibrates very, very fast when you push the on top circle. It is battery operated, and the battery is included and already installed.<br /><br />The brush is angled, so you are never pushing the brush directly into your skin. Instead, the pressure of your hand is distributed throughout the head, resulting in an even cleansing process.<br /><br />The head has blunt plastic \\"fingers\\" instead of sharp, stiff bristles, like other facial brushes. They are stiffer than a toothbrush, but less stiff than a hairbrush. They have a soft give to them, which I enjoyed. If you want that scratching, abrasion sensation, just use this brush with a scrub cleanser. The white plastic fingers are also easier to keep clean than bristles, which tend to trap or absorb dirt deep within the brush.<br /><br />There are two sizes of fingers in the head of the brush. There are smaller ones and then wide ones. The series of wide ones are arranged in two circles within the triangular head. The smaller ones fill in within and without the wider finger circles.<br /><br />The triangular shape of the whole head was great for maneuvering the angles of my face, along the sides of my nose, and along my chin especially.<br /><br />After using it, I immediately noticed a softness and brightness to my skin. I used it with a Clinique cleanser and was very pleased.<br /><br />Like all the other Vine reviewers, I did not receive the cleanser as part of my package, so I am basing my review on the brush alone.

  303. Pros: Great vibrating power, triangle brush to clean the nose, small and portable, takes one AAA battery, inexpensive<br />Cons: Not rechargeable, only lasts about a month<br /><br />Let's talk about Olay Fresh Effects since a few other people have been curious. Fresh Effects is actually a whole line, but I am most interested in their cleansing system. It comes with a vibrating wand, akin to the Olay Pro X system and the Clarisonic. However, there are a few differences that you should pay attention to.<br /><br />The Olay Pro X has a soft bristle brush head that spins and uses two double A batteries. It only comes in one model and in my experience the spinning brush head is kind of scary and makes it unusable for more than a few days a week. It's about $25 for the device and the heads do have to replace. However, since it's not as popular as the Clarisonic you can't just waltz into a Sephora and get replacements for it.<br /><br />The Clarisonic is my holy grail. A lot of people swear by this. Like the Pro X system it will clean your skin more throughly than using your hands. However, it's a bit on the pricy range, about $80-120 dollars depending on if you get it on sale. There are several models that you can get, but I currently on the Mia. This device is rechargeable (from any country without a converter), waterproof, and the bristle brush does not spin. The whole device vibrates for a timed one minute. The brush is a lot softer than those offered by the Pro X system. The power on the vibrations is fairly decent. The downside is that replacement heads cost about $20 and you have to replace them every three months with regular use.<br /><br />Now, for the Olay Fresh Effects Va-Va-Vivid cleansing system. It is a lot smaller than the Clarisonic and therefore it is a lot more portable. It's also more affordable, a cleansing system costs about $12. From my experience a wand should last you about a month if you clean it well. However, the brush head is made of a soft plastic and not a bristle. It's triangular shaped, which gets into your nose area well, but it might take a bit more work to cover your whole face.The head does not rotate, but it does vibrate. For it's size it packs quite a powerful punch. It suds up my face wash very well. I've been using it with the Shine-Go-Away that came with the set and I'm loving it. It takes one AAA battery and I don't suggest using this device regularly in the shower since I'm not sure how waterproof it is. The best part about this whole thing is that it is very portable. I used to hate carrying my Clarisonic with me on short trips since it's bulky and semi-heavy. However, this wand is super light and super small. It's effective! This makes it great for away trips. I just toss it into my makeup bag and I'm good to go!
